PUBLIC WORKS DEPARTMENT
ACQUISITION OF LANDS
FORM VI
(See Rule 16)
DECLARATION
[G.O. Ms. No. 113, Public Works (P2), 19th August 2021, ÝõE 3, Ãyt, 
ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No. II(2)/PWD/583(c-1)/2021.
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 12.93.90 hectare of land is required in the 
Vijayanarayanam Part 1 Village in Tirunelveli District in Tisayanvillai Taluk for public purpose namely 
in Interlinking of Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar, Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project.
Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 12.93.90 hectares is 
under acquisition for the above said project in the Vijayanarayanam Part 1 Village in Triunelveli District 
Tisayanvillai Taluk whose detailed description is as follows:
TAMIL NADU
GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

TOTAL
12.93.90
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation and 
Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land acquisition 
is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and minerals 
which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-5, Nanguneri and Oﬃ  ce of the Executive Engineer, Public Works 
Department, Nambiyar Reservoir Project Division, Valliyoor and Public works department on any working day.
  
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

FORM VI
[See RULE 16] 
DECLARATION
[G.O.Ms. No. 114, Public Works (P-2), 19th August 2021, ÝõE 3, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No. II(2)/PWD/583(c-2)/2021
Whereas it appears to the appropriate Government that a total of 15.50.02 hectares of land is required in the Therkku Viravanallur Part-II Village in 
Cheranmahadevi Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely Interlinking of Tamirabarani-Nambiyaru-Karumeniyar rivers for the Flood carrier canal Project. 
Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 15.50.02 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Therkku 
Viravanallur Part -II Village in Cheranmahadevi Taluk in Tirunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-1, Ambasamudram @ Cheranmahadevi and Oﬃ  ce of the 
Executive Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Tirunelveli on any working day.
    SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

DECLARATION
[G.O.Ms. No. 115, Public Works (P2), 19th August 2021, ÝõE 3, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No. II(2)/PWD/583(c-3)/2021
Whereas it appears to the appropriate Government that a total of 4.13.5 hectares of land is required in the Pudukudi Village in Cheranmahadevi Taluk in 
Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely in Inter linking of Tamirabarani-Nambiyaru-Karumeniyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project. Now, therefore a 
declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 4.13.5 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Pudukudi Village in Cheranmahadevi 
Taluk in Triunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

4.13.5
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under Section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-1, Ambasamudram @ Cheranmahadevi and Oﬃ  ce of the 
Executive Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Nanguneri on any working day.
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

FORM VI
[See Rule 16] 
DECLARATION
[G.O.Ms. No. 116, Public Works (P2), 19th August 2021, ÝõE 3, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No. II(2)/PWD/583(c-4)/2021
Whereas it appears to the appropriate Government that a total of 3.88.99 hectares of land is required in the Therkku Viravanallur Part - I Village in 
Cheranmahadevi Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely in Inter linking of Tamirabarani- Nambiyaru - Karumeniyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal 
Project.Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 3.88.99 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Therkku 
Viravanallur Part - I Village in Cheranmahadevi Taluk in Triunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-1, Ambasamudram @ Cheranmahadevi and Oﬃ  ce of the 
Executive Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Nanguneri, on any working day.
 
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

65
FORM VI
[See Rule 16] 
DECLARATION
[G.O.Ms. No. 117, Public Works (P2) Dept, 19th August 2021, ÝõE 3, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No.II(2)/PWD/583(c-5)/2021
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 25.57.40 hectares of land is required in the Vijayanarayanam Part 3 Village in Tirunelveli District in 
Tisayanvillai Taluk for public purpose namely in Interlinking of Tamirabarani - Karumeniyar - Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project.Now, therefore a 
declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 25.57.40 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Vijayanarayanam Part 1 Village 
Stage 3 in Triunelveli District Tisayanvillai Taluk whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-5, Nanguneri and Oﬃ  ce of the Executive Engineer, Public 
Works Department, Nambiyar Reservoir Project Division, Vallioor on any working day. 
 
SANDEEP SAXENA,  
 
 
 
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-6, Radhapuram @ Nanguneri and Oﬃ  ce of the Executive 
Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Ambasamuthiram and Public works department ,Special project Sub Division -2, Moolaikaraipatti on any 
working day.
 
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY 
129
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-6, Radhapuram @ Nanguneri and Oﬃ  ce of the Executive 
Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Ambasamuthiram and Public works department ,Special projectsub Sub Division -2, Moolaikaraipatti on 
any working day.
  
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

FORM VI

DECLARATION
[G.O.Ms. No. 119, Public Works (P2), 19th August 2021, ÝõE 3, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No.II(2)/PWD/583(c-7)/2021
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 4.26.61 hectares of land is required in the Kovankulam Village in Thisayanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli 
District for public purpose namely in Interlinking of Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project. Now, therefore a declaration is 
made hereby that a piece of land measuring 4.26.61 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Kovankulam Village in Thisayanvilai Taluk in 
Triunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under Section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-6, Radhapuram @ Nanguneri and Oﬃ  ce of the Executive 
Engineer, Public Works Department, Nambiyar Reservoir Project Division, Valliyoor on any working day.
  
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
FORM VI
[See Rule 16] 
DECLARATION
[G.O.Ms. No. 120, Public Works (P2), 19th August 2021, ÝõE 3, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No.II(2)/PWD/583(c-8)/2021
Whereas it appears to the appropriate Government that a total of 16.08.81 hectares of land is required in the Mela Seval Part - II Village in Cheranmahadevi 
Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely in Inter linking of Tamirabarani-Nambiyaru-Karumeniyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project. Now, therefore 
a declaration is made hereby that a piece of land measuring 16.08.81 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the MelaSeval Part - II Village 
in Cheranmahadevi Taluk in Tirunelveli District whose detailed description is as follows:

16.08.81
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-1, Ambasamudram @ Cheranmahadevi and Oﬃ  ce of the 
Executive Engineer, Public Works Department, Special Project Division, Nanguneri on any working day.
 
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.

FORM VI
[See Rule 16] 
DECLARATION
[G.O.Ms. No. 121, Public Works (P2), 19th August 2021, ÝõE 3, Ãyt, ÂUtŸSt® M©L-2052.]
No.II(2)/PWD/583(c-9)/2021
Whereas it appears to the Government that a total of 30.92.74 hectares of land is required in the Ilankulam Village in Nanguneri Taluk in Tirunelveli District for 
public purpose namely in Interlinking of Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar rivers for the Flood Carrier Canal Project.Now, therefore a declaration is made hereby 
that a piece of land measuring 30.92.74 hectares is under acquisition for the above said project in the Ilankulam Village in Nanguneri Taluk in Triunelveli District 
whose detailed description is as follows:

196 
TAMIL  NADU  GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE  EXTRAORDINARY
This declaration is made after hearing of objections of persons interested and due enquiry as provided under section 15 of the Right to Fair Compensation 
and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013). The number of families likely to be resettled due to land 
acquisition is Nil.
Mines of coal, iron-stone, slate or other minerals lying under the said land or any particular portion of the said land, except such parts of the mines and 
minerals which may be required to be dug or removed or used during the construction phase of the project for the purpose of which the land is being acquired, 
are not needed.
A plan of the land may be inspected in the Oﬃ  ce of the Special Tahsildar, River Linking Project, Unit-6, Radhapuram @ Nanguneri and  Oﬃ  ce of the Executive 
Engineer, Public Works Department, Nambiyar Reservoir Project Division, Valliyoor on any working day.
 
 
SANDEEP SAXENA,
 
 
Additional Chief Secretary to Government.
